<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выращивать.html>выра́щивать</a> (10972)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырастить.html>вы́растить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výrastitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выращивать.html>выра́щивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyráščivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырастить.html>вы́растить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grow, to raise, to cultivate</li>
<li>to breed, to rear, to raise</li>
<li>to bring up</li>
<li>to train, to prepare, to form</li></ol>

***вырвать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вырвать.html>вы́рвать</a> (3120)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырвать.html>вы́рвать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výrvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырывать.html>вырыва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pull out</li>
<li>to tear out</li>
<li>to snatch out <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">from someone's hands</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to pull up (a plant)</li>
<li>to eradicate, to extirpate, to root out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to extort, to wring, to wrest</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to vomit
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вырвать.html>вы́рвало</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó <b>výrvalo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he vomited</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырываться.html>вырыва́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vyryvátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вырваться.html>вы́рваться</a> (2240)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырвать.html>вы́рвать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výrvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырваться.html>вы́рваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výrvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырываться.html>вырыва́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to break away, to break loose, to escape</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to escape (words, sound, moan, etc.)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырвать.html>вы́рвать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výrvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***вырез.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вырез.html>вы́рез</a> (17656)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырез.html>вы́рез</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výrez</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырез.html>вы́реза</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырез.html>вы́резы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырез.html>вы́резов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cut, cutting</li>
<li>cutout</li>
<li>low neck, decollete</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> excision</li></ol>

***вырезать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вырезать.html>выреза́ть</a> (4349)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резать.html>ре́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rézatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырезать.html>вы́резать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výrezatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырезать.html>выреза́ть</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">выре́зывать</b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the impf./pf. forms differ in the word stress in the infinitive and the conjugation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to carve, to engrave</li>
<li>to cut out, to excise</li>
<li>to massacre, to slaughter, to butcher
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырезать.html>выреза́ть</a></strong></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vyrezátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">only</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырезать.html>вы́резать</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výrezatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырезать.html>выреза́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyrezátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырезать.html>вы́резать</a></strong></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the impf./pf. forms differ in the word stress in the infinitive and the conjugation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to carve, to engrave</li>
<li>to cut out, to excise</li>
<li>to massacre, to slaughter, to butcher</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырезать.html>вы́резать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výrezatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырезка.html>вы́резка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výrezka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырезка.html>вы́резки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырезка.html>вы́резки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырезка.html>вы́резок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cutting out, engraving, carving</li>
<li>press cutting, press clipping</li>
<li>undercut, sirloin, fillet, tenderloin</li></ol>

***вырисовываться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вырисовываться.html>вырисо́вываться</a> (14526)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вырисо́вывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vyrisóvyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырисовываться.html>вырисо́вываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyrisóvyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вы́рисоваться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to come into sight/view, to loom, to appear, to come into the picture
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вырисовываться.html>вырисо́вываться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фон.html>фо́не</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyrisóvyvatʹsja</b> na fóne</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stand out (against); stand out in relief (against)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:горизонт.html>горизо́нте</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вырисовываться.html>вырисо́вывалась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:горный.html>го́рная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цепь.html>цепь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na gorizónte <b>vyrisóvyvalasʹ</b> górnaja cepʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a mountain chain was visible on [stood out against] the <a href = vnd.unilang:горизонт.html>horizon</a></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдали.html>вдали́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:начать.html>начал</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вырисовываться.html>вырисо́вываться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:корабль.html>кора́бль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vdalí načal <b>vyrisóvyvatʹsja</b> koráblʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a ship loomed in the distance</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to become clearer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сейчас.html>сейча́с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вырисовываться.html>вырисо́вывается</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:картина.html>карти́на</a> происше́дшего</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sejčás <b>vyrisóvyvajetsja</b> kartína proisšédševo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the detailed picture of the incident is being completed now</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take shape, to emerge, to develop
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нас</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вырисовываться.html>вырисо́вывается</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:план.html>план</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nas <b>vyrisóvyvajetsja</b> odín plan</i> ― <span class="e-translation">we are making/developing a certain plan</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вырисовываться.html>вырисо́вывается</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:завтра.html>за́втра</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">što tam <b>vyrisóvyvajetsja</b> na závtra?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">what plans do we have for tomorrow?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вырисо́вывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vyrisóvyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выровнять.html>вы́ровнять</a> (25483)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ровнять.html>ровня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rovnjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выровнять.html>вы́ровнять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výrovnjatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выравнивать.html>выра́внивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to (make) even, to smooth out, to make level</li>
<li>to flatten (out)</li>
<li>to iron out (differences)</li>
<li>to align, to line up <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to adjust or form to a line</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выровнять.html>вы́ровнять</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́вому</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:край.html>кра́ю</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výrovnjatʹ</b> po právomu kráju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to right-<b>align</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to equalize</li>
<li>to justify (e.g. text on a page)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выродиться.html>вы́родиться</a> (28152)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́родить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výroditʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to (cause to) degenerate <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выродиться.html>вы́родиться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výroditʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырождаться.html>вырожда́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to degenerate</li>
<li>to disappear, to be lost over time</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вырождавшийся.html>вырожда́вшийся</a> (28170)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырождавшийся.html>вырожда́вшийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyroždávšijsja</span>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вырожда́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vyroždátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to (cause to) degenerate <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырождаться.html>вырожда́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyroždátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выродиться.html>вы́родиться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to degenerate</li>
<li>to disappear, to be lost over time</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вырождающийся.html>вырожда́ющийся</a> (28170)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***вырубать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вырубать.html>выруба́ть</a> (21623)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырубить.html>вы́рубить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výrubitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырубать.html>выруба́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyrubátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырубить.html>вы́рубить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cut down, to fell</li>
<li>to cut out</li>
<li><i>(hole, window etc)</i> to make</li>
<li><i>(ore, coal)</i> to cut, to hew</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn off, to switch off, to cut off</li></ol>

***вырубить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вырубить.html>вы́рубить</a> (9134)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рубить.html>руби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rubítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырубить.html>вы́рубить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výrubitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырубать.html>выруба́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cut down, to fell</li>
<li>to cut out</li>
<li><i>(hole, window etc)</i> to make</li>
<li><i>(ore, coal)</i> to cut, to hew</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn off, to switch off, to cut off</li></ol>

***выругаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выругаться.html>вы́ругаться</a> (5901)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выругать.html>вы́ругать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výrugatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выругаться.html>вы́ругаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výrugatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to swear, to curse, to use bad language, to call names</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выругать.html>вы́ругать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výrugatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вы́браниться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výbranitʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ругнуться.html>ругну́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rugnútʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ругательный.html>руга́тельный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rugátelʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***выручать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выручать.html>выруча́ть</a> (8305)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выручить.html>вы́ручить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výručitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выручать.html>выруча́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyručátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выручить.html>вы́ручить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rescue, to come to somebody's help/aid/assistance
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выручать.html>выруча́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:беда.html>беды́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyručátʹ</b> kovó-libo iz bedý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to help somebody out of trouble; to hold out a helping hand to somebody</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выручать.html>выруча́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плена.html>пле́на</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyručátʹ</b> iz pléna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to deliver/release smb from captivity</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выручка.html>вы́ручка</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výručka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***выручить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выручить.html>вы́ручить</a> (5346)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выручить.html>вы́ручить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výručitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выручать.html>выруча́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rescue, to come to smb's help/aid/assistance
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выручить.html>вы́ручи</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:получка.html>полу́чки</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výruči</b> menjá do polúčki</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">lend me some money till the payday</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сто.html>сто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубле́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:выручить.html>вы́ручат</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sto rubléj menjá ne <b>výručat</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">a hundred roubles won't save me</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make, to gain, to net, to clear
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выручить.html>вы́ручить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:затраченный.html>затра́ченное</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výručitʹ</b> zatráčennoje</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to recover one's expenses</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
